data-testid="Placeholder" class="jsx-3144213232 Placeholder Figure__placeholder"></div><div data-testid="Placeholder" class="jsx-5562127 Placeholder Figure__placeholder"></div></div><div class="jsx-3236492107 jsx-4058332174 Figure__image-info"><figcaption class="jsx-1605011749 jsx-1422938156 ImageCaption"><div class="jsx-1605011749 jsx-1422938156 ImageCaption__credit"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html">Credit: Photo: Alex Lepe; Food Styling: Janette Zepeda</div></div></figcaption></div></figure></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><p>If you’re looking for a way to make <a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/20-minute-weeknight-dinner-recipes-23655506">weeknight dinners</a> more exciting without too much effort, consider <a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/collection/recipe/sauce">adding a sauce</a>. I’ve been making this “sunshine sauce” on repeat all winter long. Sunshine sauce is a citrus-y take on the classic French butter sauce <a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/the-secret-2-ingredient-butter-sauce-you-need-to-know-about-228872">beurre monté</a>. This recipe takes just 15 minutes and needs only 4 ingredients — ingredients that I always have on hand. Sunshine sauce is incredibly easy to make: Just whisk pats of cold butter into warm lemon juice until the sauce is rich and creamy, and finish with garlic and parsley. Here’s how to make it. </p></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__ad"><div data-size-label="post-small" class="jsx-2289411083 Ad Ad--6782-GenKitchn-Post-Post_002 Ad--empty"><div data-ay-manager-id="post" id="dfp-post-002-0" data-ad-unit-path="/6782/GenKitchn/Post/Post_002" data-size-mapping="{&quot;sizeMapping&quot;:[{&quot;viewport&quot;:[0,0],&quot;slot&quot;:[[300,250],[400,300],[1,1]]},{&quot;viewport&quot;:[1024,0],&quot;slot&quot;:[]}]}" data-ppid-allowed="true" class="jsx-2289411083"></div></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__heading Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><h2 class="wp-block-heading">Why You’ll Love It</h2></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>There’s just 4 ingredients. </strong>With just lemon, butter, parsley, and garlic (plus kosher salt and pepper, which we consider freebies), you can make a restaurant-quality sauce that is full of flavor.</li>



<li><strong>It’s so versatile. </strong>There’s no shortage of ways to serve this buttery lemon sauce. You can use it as a dipping sauce for meats and seafood, drizzled over vegetables, or tossed with pasta or potatoes. </li>
</ul></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__inPostVideoAdDesktop Post__related"><div class="jsx-93529230 cnx-container-in-post-desktop"><div class="lazyload-wrapper "><div class="lazyload-placeholder"></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__image"><figure data-testid="Figure" class="jsx-3236492107 jsx-4058332174 Figure"><div class="jsx-3236492107 jsx-4058332174 Figure__image"><div class="lazyload-wrapper "><div class="lazyload-placeholder"></div></div><div data-testid="Placeholder" class="jsx-554496548 Placeholder Figure__placeholder"></div><div data-testid="Placeholder" class="jsx-3799123675 Placeholder Figure__placeholder"></div><noscript><img src="https://cdn.apartmenttherapy.info/image/upload/f_auto,q_auto:eco,w_730/k%2FPhoto%2FRecipes%2F2025-05-sunshine-sauce%2FWC-sunshine-sauce-178-vertical" alt="sunshine sauce on a plate with chicken"/></noscript></div><div class="jsx-3236492107 jsx-4058332174 Figure__image-info"><figcaption class="jsx-1605011749 jsx-1422938156 ImageCaption"><div class="jsx-1605011749 jsx-1422938156 ImageCaption__credit"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html">Credit: Photo: Alex Lepe; Food Styling: Janette Zepeda</div></div></figcaption></div></figure></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__heading Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><h2 class="wp-block-heading">Key Ingredients in Sunshine Sauce</h2></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>Lemon: </strong>Fresh lemon is the star of the sauce. Use a <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Microplane-40020-Classic-Zester-Grater/dp/B00004S7V8/ref=asc_df_B00004S7V8?asc_campaign=KT-23706247&amp;asc_refurl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.thekitchn.com%2Fsunshine-sauce-recipe-23706247&amp;asc_source=%7BREFERRAL_SOURCE%7D&amp;tag=kitchn-20" data-product-id="TextLinkProduct:6019543152459776" data-link-type="product" rel="noopener nofollow sponsored" target="_blank" class="product-link" data-gtm-teaser-product-id="TextLinkProduct:6019543152459776" data-gtm-teaser-product-name="[PLACEHOLDER NAME]" data-gtm-teaser-product-retailers="Amazon" data-gtm-teaser-product-url="https://www.amazon.com/Microplane-40020-Classic-Zester-Grater/dp/B00004S7V8/ref=asc_df_B00004S7V8" data-gtm-trigger="element-visible click" data-gtm-event-category="ecommerce" data-gtm-ui-component="post_product_text_link">Microplane to finely grate</a> the zest and a <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Chefn-FreshForce-Citrus-Juicer-Lemon/dp/B002XOB0P0/ref=sr_1_19?asc_campaign=KT-23706247&amp;asc_refurl=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.thekitchn.com%2Fsunshine-sauce-recipe-23706247&amp;asc_source=%7BREFERRAL_SOURCE%7D&amp;tag=kitchn-20" data-product-id="TextLinkProduct:5074720769703936" data-link-type="product" rel="noopener nofollow sponsored" target="_blank" class="product-link" data-gtm-teaser-product-id="TextLinkProduct:5074720769703936" data-gtm-teaser-product-name="[PLACEHOLDER NAME]" data-gtm-teaser-product-retailers="Amazon" data-gtm-teaser-product-url="https://www.amazon.com/Chefn-FreshForce-Citrus-Juicer-Lemon/dp/B002XOB0P0/ref=sr_1_19" data-gtm-trigger="element-visible click" data-gtm-event-category="ecommerce" data-gtm-ui-component="post_product_text_link">citrus juicer</a> to squeeze out the tart juice. </li>



<li><strong>Unsalted butter: </strong>This sauce is built on butter. With so few ingredients, use the best butter you can. Go for <a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/whats-the-difference-between-european-and-american-butter-229135">European-style butters</a> like Kerrygold, which often have a higher butterfat content and richer color. </li>



<li><strong>Garlic: </strong>One minced garlic clove lends subtle flavor to the sauce, but garlic lovers may want to add an extra clove.   </li>



<li><strong>Parsley: </strong>Stir chopped fresh parsley in just before serving to infuse the butter sauce with fresh flavor without wilting the herbs.</li>
</ul></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__heading Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><h2 class="wp-block-heading">What to Serve with Sunshine Sauce</h2></div></div><div data-testid="Post__item" class="jsx-2588235784 jsx-1035508318 Post__item Post__html"><div data-testid="base-html" class="Html"><ul class="wp-block-list">

<li><a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/how-to-quickly-cook-shrimp-on-the-stovetop-cooking-lessons-from-the-kitchn-214397">Roasted Brussels Sprouts</a></li>



<li><a href="https://www.thekitchn.com/how-to-cook-perfect-salmon-fillets-230150">Pan-Seared Salmon</a></li>

as Kerrygold, cut into 8 pieces</p></span></span></li><li class="Recipe__ingredient" data-testid="ingredient"><span class="Recipe__ingredientQuantity">1 </span><span class="Recipe__ingredientMeasurementUnit">teaspoon </span><span class="Recipe__ingredientName"><p>freshly ground black pepper, plus more as needed</p></span></span></li></ul></div></div><div class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__ingredientsAddOn"><div class="lazyload-wrapper "><div style="height:0" class="lazyload-placeholder"></div></div></div></section><section class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__instructionsSection"><div class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__instructionsHeader"><h3 class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__instructionsHeading">Instructions</h3></div><div class="Recipe__instructionsGroups"><div class="Recipe__instructionsGroup" data-testid="Recipe__instructionsGroup" id="instructions-731280320-instructiongroup-1"><ol class="Recipe__instructions"><li class="Recipe__instructionStep" data-testid="Recipe__instructionStep"><div id="step-731280320-instructiongroup-1-1" class="Recipe__instructionStepContent"><span><p>Bring 1 tablespoon plus 1 teaspoon lemon juice and 1 tablespoon water to a simmer in a small skillet or saucepan over medium-low heat. Reduce the heat to low. Whisk in 1 stick cold unsalted butter a tablespoon at a time, whisking until each piece is almost melted before adding the next. Do not let the butter boil, or it will separate.</p></span></div></li><li class="Recipe__instructionStep" data-testid="Recipe__instructionStep"><div id="step-731280320-instructiongroup-1-2" class="Recipe__instructionStepContent"><span><p>Whisk in 1 teaspoon finely grated lemon zest, 1 tablespoon coarsely chopped fresh parsley leaves, 1 minced garlic clove, 1/4 teaspoon kosher salt, and 1/4 teaspoon black pepper. Taste and season with more kosher salt or black pepper as needed. Serve warm.</p></span></div></li></ol></div></div></section><section class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__notesSection"><h3 class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__notesHeading">Recipe Notes</h3><div class="jsx-1572587876 Recipe__notes"><p><strong>Storage: </strong>This butter sauce is best made right before serving, but you can refrigerate leftover butter in an airtight container for up to 4 days. Reheat in a small saucepan over low heat until completely melted and warm; do not let it boil. Remove from the heat. Drizzle in cool water 1 teaspoon at a time while whisking vigorously, until the sauce is creamy and emulsified again.</p><p>The butter sauce can also be used cold: Toss with hot pasta, boiled potatoes, or cooked green beans for an instant flavor boost.</p></div></section></div></div><div class="jsx-2056869793 jsx-2650934534 Post__recipeRoundupRecirc
